        </div><div class="casAbstract">A Na3V2(PO4)3/C (NVP/C) composite is successfully synthesized by sol-gel method and examd. as an anode material for sodium-ion batteries by means of galvanostatic charge-discharge profiles, cyclic voltammetry, rate performance and cyclic voltammetry comprehensively.  The NVP/C electrode delivers a reversible capacity of about 170 mA-h/g between 3.0 and 0.01 V at a c.d. of 20 mA/g corresponding to three sodium ions insertion/extn. processes.  Besides the voltage plateau at 1.57 V, another novel working platform at around 0.28 V is found for the first time in both charging and discharging profiles, possibly owing to the further redn. of vanadium.  NVP/C exhibits an excellent rate capability and long-cycle stability with a capacity retention of 62% after 3000 cycles at a high charge rate of 10C (2 A/g).  Moreover, the intercalation-type Na-ions storage mechanism is proposed on the basis of ex situ x-ray diffraction and high-resoln. transmission electron microscopy.  Our findings reveal that the NVP/C sample is a promising anode material for sodium-ion batteries due to its superior rate capability and long cycle life.</div></div><div class="moreSciFi"><a title="Retrieve detailed record, substances, reactions and more for this article from SciFinder ®" href="https://scifinder.cas.org/scifinder/view/link_v1/reference.jsf?l=BmxxGlm8wGp9kPnWXbnJvLVg90H21EOLACvtfcHk0lgw1kg31UJJPg"> &gt;&gt; More from SciFinder <sup>®</sup></a></div><span class="casRefUrl">https://chemport.cas.org/services/resolver?origin=ACS&amp;resolution=options&amp;coi=1%3ACAS%3A528%3ADC%252BC2MXks1ejsrs%253D&amp;md5=585f5caf6996cceca1c4b7c5337eaa0d</span></div></div></div></div></li><li id="rightTab-ref42"><div class="reference"><strong class="refLabel"><a href="#ref42" class="rightTabRefNumLink">42</a></strong><div class="NLM_citation references__item" id="rightTab-cit42" data-doi="10.1039/C5TA00765H"><span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Wang, Q.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Zhao, B.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Zhang, S.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Gao, X.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Deng, C.</span><span> </span><span class="NLM_article-title">Superior sodium intercalation of honeycomb-structured hierarchical porous Na3V2(PO4)3/C microballs prepared by a facile one-pot synthesis</span> <span class="citation_source-journal">J. Mater. Chem. A</span><span class="NLM_x"> </span><span class="NLM_year" style="font-weight: bold;">2015</span><span class="NLM_x">, </span> <span class="NLM_volume">3</span><span class="NLM_x"> (</span><span class="NLM_issue">15</span><span class="NLM_x">) </span> <span class="NLM_fpage">7732</span><span class="NLM_x">–</span> <span class="NLM_lpage">7740</span><span class="refDoi">&nbsp;DOI:
                10.1039/C5TA00765H</span> </span><div class=" links-group getFTR"><div class="getFTR__content getFTR__placeholder"></div><div class="casRecord" id="
                        rightTab-cas_cit42R"><div class="casContent"><span class="casTitleNuber">42</span><div class="casTitle"><span class="NLM_cas:atitle">Superior sodium intercalation of honeycomb-structured hierarchical porous Na3V2(PO4)3/C microballs prepared by a facile one-pot synthesis</span></div><div class="casAuthors">Wang, Qiuyue; Zhao, Baidan; Zhang, Sen; Gao, Xiaohui; Deng, Chao</div><div class="citationInfo"><span class="NLM_cas:title">Journal of Materials Chemistry A: Materials for Energy and Sustainability</span>
        (<span class="NLM_cas:date">2015</span>),
    <span class="NLM_cas:volume">3</span>
        (<span class="NLM_cas:issue">15</span>),
    <span class="NLM_cas:pages">7732-7740</span>CODEN:
                <span class="NLM_cas:coden">JMCAET</span>;
        ISSN:<span class="NLM_cas:issn">2050-7496</span>.
    
            (<span class="NLM_cas:orgname">Royal Society of Chemistry</span>)
        </div><div class="casAbstract">Tailoring materials into a hierarchical porous microstructure/nanostructure offers unprecedented opportunities in the utilization of their functional properties.  Particularly, it is crucial for the electrode materials to realize high-performance because of the advantages such as large surface area, superior structure stability and short ion transport pathway.  Here we report the design of a new architecture, named "honeycomb-type hierarchical porous microball", for Na3V2(PO4)3 by a facile one-pot synthesis.  The network between nanovoids is formed by in situ carbonization of surfactants cetyltrimethylammonium bromide along with the crystn. of Na3V2(PO4)3, which results in the hierarchical porous Na3V2(PO4)3 skeleton with a surface conductive layer.  The prepd. Na3V2(PO4)3/C composite consists of spherical particles filled with hierarchical pores and interconnective nanochannels, resulting in the honeycomb-type architecture.  It not only enables easier electrolyte penetration, but also provides a high-efficiency electron/ion transport pathway for fast sodium intercalation.  Both the GITT and EIS results demonstrate the improved sodium diffusion capability and decreased electrochem. resistance for the honeycomb-structured microball in comparison to the microsized nonporous ref. samples.  Moreover, it also delivers superior high rate capability and cycling stability, which retains 93.6% of the initial capacity after 200 cycles at the 1C rate.  Even at 20C, it still delivers a high capacity of 80.2 mA-h/g corresponding to 71% of the capacity.  Given the superior ion intercalation kinetics and excellent structure stability, the honeycomb-type structure puts forward a new strategy to develop high-performance polyanion-based materials for low-cost and high-power rocking-chair batteries.</div></div><div class="moreSciFi"><a title="Retrieve detailed record, substances, reactions and more for this article from SciFinder ®" href="https://scifinder.cas.org/scifinder/view/link_v1/reference.jsf?l=BmxxGlm8wGpvZ5alxiDtgLVg90H21EOLACvtfcHk0lgw1kg31UJJPg"> &gt;&gt; More from SciFinder <sup>®</sup></a></div><span class="casRefUrl">https://chemport.cas.org/services/resolver?origin=ACS&amp;resolution=options&amp;coi=1%3ACAS%3A528%3ADC%252BC2MXjtVynu7s%253D&amp;md5=f5729fed5eb9dabc461297140bc161c5</span></div></div></div></div></li><li id="rightTab-ref43"><div class="reference"><strong class="refLabel"><a href="#ref43" class="rightTabRefNumLink">43</a></strong><div class="NLM_citation references__item" id="rightTab-cit43" data-doi="10.1016/j.ceramint.2015.09.003"><span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Chu, Z.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Yue, C.</span><span> </span><span class="NLM_article-title">Graphene oxide wrapped Na3V2(PO4)3/C nanocomposite as superior cathode material for sodium-ion batteries</span> <span class="citation_source-journal">Ceram. Int.</span><span class="NLM_x"> </span><span class="NLM_year" style="font-weight: bold;">2016</span><span class="NLM_x">, </span> <span class="NLM_volume">42</span><span class="NLM_x"> (</span><span class="NLM_issue">1</span><span class="NLM_x">) </span> <span class="NLM_fpage">820</span><span class="NLM_x">–</span> <span class="NLM_lpage">827</span><span class="refDoi">&nbsp;DOI:
                10.1016/j.ceramint.2015.09.003</span> </span><div class=" links-group getFTR"><div class="getFTR__content getFTR__placeholder"></div><div class="casRecord" id="
                        rightTab-cas_cit43R"><div class="casContent"><span class="casTitleNuber">43</span><div class="casTitle"><span class="NLM_cas:atitle">Graphene oxide wrapped Na3V2(PO4)3/C nanocomposite as superior cathode material for sodium-ion batteries</span></div><div class="casAuthors">Chu, Zhaolian; Yue, Caibo</div><div class="citationInfo"><span class="NLM_cas:title">Ceramics International</span>
        (<span class="NLM_cas:date">2016</span>),
    <span class="NLM_cas:volume">42</span>
        (<span class="NLM_cas:issue">1_Part_A</span>),
    <span class="NLM_cas:pages">820-827</span>CODEN:
                <span class="NLM_cas:coden">CINNDH</span>;
        ISSN:<span class="NLM_cas:issn">0272-8842</span>.
    
            (<span class="NLM_cas:orgname">Elsevier Ltd.</span>)
        </div><div class="casAbstract">Na3V2(PO4)3 is one of the most promising cathode materials for rechargeable sodium-ion batteries, which can deliver two Na+ ions extn./insertion from/into the crystal structure.  To further improve the electrochem. performance of the carbon-coated Na3V2(PO4)3 electrode, the conducting graphene has been adopted.  In this paper, graphene-wrapped Na3V2(PO4)3/C nanocomposite has been successfully synthesized through a hydrothermal-assisted sol-gel method.  X-ray diffraction (XRD) results demonstrate that the obtained nanocomposite is well crystd. with NASICON-type structure.  The SEM (SEM) and transmission electron microscopy (TEM) images reveal that the modification of Na3V2(PO4)3/C with graphene could construct an effective conducting network, which significantly enhances the electronic cond. of Na3V2(PO4)3/C based sample.  Thus, the graphene-wrapped Na3V2(PO4)3/C exhibits superior high-rate capacity and excellent cycling stability.  It shows an initial charge capacity of 113 mA h g-1 and a discharge capacity of 106.5 mA h g-1 at 0.1 C, and retains stable discharge capacities of 104.3, 101.1, 96.4 and 93 mA h g-1 at current rates of 0.2 C, 0.5 C, 1 C and 2 C, resp.  Even at higher rate of 5 C, it can still deliver a discharge capacity of 88.7 mA h g-1 with remarkable capacity retention of 92.5% after 200 cycles.  This synthetic strategy should be helpful for the design of other conducting network structured electrodes with high-performances.</div></div><div class="moreSciFi"><a title="Retrieve detailed record, substances, reactions and more for this article from SciFinder ®" href="https://scifinder.cas.org/scifinder/view/link_v1/reference.jsf?l=BmxxGlm8wGoHTBKHXrHNOLVg90H21EOLACvtfcHk0lgw1kg31UJJPg"> &gt;&gt; More from SciFinder <sup>®</sup></a></div><span class="casRefUrl">https://chemport.cas.org/services/resolver?origin=ACS&amp;resolution=options&amp;coi=1%3ACAS%3A528%3ADC%252BC2MXhsFajtb3N&amp;md5=209a15e88d1e68a9a5e94da860f2ec0c</span></div></div></div></div></li><li id="rightTab-ref44"><div class="reference"><strong class="refLabel"><a href="#ref44" class="rightTabRefNumLink">44</a></strong><div class="NLM_citation references__item" id="rightTab-cit44" data-doi="10.1039/C5TA08869K"><span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Fang, J.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Wang, S.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Li, Z.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Chen, H.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Xia, L.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Ding, L.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Wang, H.</span><span> </span><span class="NLM_article-title">Porous Na3V2(PO4)3@C nanoparticles enwrapped in three-dimensional graphene for high performance sodium-ion batteries</span> <span class="citation_source-journal">J. Mater. Chem. A</span><span class="NLM_x"> </span><span class="NLM_year" style="font-weight: bold;">2016</span><span class="NLM_x">, </span> <span class="NLM_volume">4</span><span class="NLM_x"> (</span><span class="NLM_issue">4</span><span class="NLM_x">) </span> <span class="NLM_fpage">1180</span><span class="NLM_x">–</span> <span class="NLM_lpage">1185</span><span class="refDoi">&nbsp;DOI:
                10.1039/C5TA08869K</span> </span><div class=" links-group getFTR"><div class="getFTR__content getFTR__placeholder"></div><div class="casRecord" id="
                        rightTab-cas_cit44R"><div class="casContent"><span class="casTitleNuber">44</span><div class="casTitle"><span class="NLM_cas:atitle">Porous Na3V2(PO4)3@C nanoparticles enwrapped in three-dimensional graphene for high performance sodium-ion batteries</span></div><div class="casAuthors">Fang, Junqi; Wang, Suqing; Li, Zhitong; Chen, Hongbin; Xia, Lu; Ding, Liangxin; Wang, Haihui</div><div class="citationInfo"><span class="NLM_cas:title">Journal of Materials Chemistry A: Materials for Energy and Sustainability</span>
        (<span class="NLM_cas:date">2016</span>),
    <span class="NLM_cas:volume">4</span>
        (<span class="NLM_cas:issue">4</span>),
    <span class="NLM_cas:pages">1180-1185</span>CODEN:
                <span class="NLM_cas:coden">JMCAET</span>;
        ISSN:<span class="NLM_cas:issn">2050-7496</span>.
    
            (<span class="NLM_cas:orgname">Royal Society of Chemistry</span>)
        </div><div class="casAbstract">Porous Na3V2(PO4)3@C nanocomposites enwrapped in a 3D graphene network were prepd. using a simple freeze-drying-assisted thermal treatment method.  The carbon layer and 3D graphene network provide not only a 3D conductive network but also a double restriction on the aggregation of Na3V2(PO4)3 particles that have a high crystallinity under high temp. treatment.  Due to the high electrochem. activity of the highly cryst. Na3V2(PO4)3 nanoparticles and 3D conductive network, the novel NVP@C/G material displays a superior rate capability (76 mA h g-1 at 60C) and ultra-long cyclability (82% capacity retention for 1500 cycles at 40C) when used in sodium-ion batteries.</div></div><div class="moreSciFi"><a title="Retrieve detailed record, substances, reactions and more for this article from SciFinder ®" href="https://scifinder.cas.org/scifinder/view/link_v1/reference.jsf?l=BmxxGlm8wGq_NG0gB9T_PLVg90H21EOLACvtfcHk0lgw1kg31UJJPg"> &gt;&gt; More from SciFinder <sup>®</sup></a></div><span class="casRefUrl">https://chemport.cas.org/services/resolver?origin=ACS&amp;resolution=options&amp;coi=1%3ACAS%3A528%3ADC%252BC2MXhvFWqt7rP&amp;md5=70d3e402ff571ebc4953b11f3a77eb0f</span></div></div></div></div></li><li id="rightTab-ref45"><div class="reference"><strong class="refLabel"><a href="#ref45" class="rightTabRefNumLink">45</a></strong><div class="NLM_citation references__item" id="rightTab-cit45" data-doi="10.1039/C3EE42944J"><span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Wu, L.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Hu, X. H.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Qian, J. F.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Pei, F.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Wu, F. Y.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Mao, R. J.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Ai, X. P.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Yang, H. X.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Cao, Y. L.</span><span> </span><span class="NLM_article-title">Sb-C nanofibers with long cycle life as an anode material for high-performance sodium-ion batteries</span> <span class="citation_source-journal">Energy Environ. Sci.</span><span class="NLM_x"> </span><span class="NLM_year" style="font-weight: bold;">2014</span><span class="NLM_x">, </span> <span class="NLM_volume">7</span><span class="NLM_x"> (</span><span class="NLM_issue">1</span><span class="NLM_x">) </span> <span class="NLM_fpage">323</span><span class="NLM_x">–</span> <span class="NLM_lpage">328</span><span class="refDoi">&nbsp;DOI:
                10.1039/C3EE42944J</span> </span><div class=" links-group getFTR"><div class="getFTR__content getFTR__placeholder"></div><div class="casRecord" id="
                        rightTab-cas_cit45R"><div class="casContent"><span class="casTitleNuber">45</span><div class="casTitle"><span class="NLM_cas:atitle">Sb-C nanofibers with long cycle life as an anode material for high-performance sodium-ion batteries</span></div><div class="casAuthors">Wu, Lin; Hu, Xiaohong; Qian, Jiangfeng; Pei, Feng; Wu, Fayuan; Mao, Rongjun; Ai, Xinping; Yang, Hanxi; Cao, Yuliang</div><div class="citationInfo"><span class="NLM_cas:title">Energy &amp; Environmental Science</span>
        (<span class="NLM_cas:date">2014</span>),
    <span class="NLM_cas:volume">7</span>
        (<span class="NLM_cas:issue">1</span>),
    <span class="NLM_cas:pages">323-328</span>CODEN:
                <span class="NLM_cas:coden">EESNBY</span>;
        ISSN:<span class="NLM_cas:issn">1754-5706</span>.
    
            (<span class="NLM_cas:orgname">Royal Society of Chemistry</span>)
        </div><div class="casAbstract">Sb-C nanofibers are synthesized successfully through a single-nozzle electrospinning technique and subsequent calcination.  The structural and morphol. characterizations reveal the uniform nanofiber structure with the Sb nanoparticles embedded homogeneously in the carbon nanofibers.  Electrochem. expts. show that the Sb-C nanofiber electrode can deliver large reversible capacity (631 mA h g-1) at C/15, greatly improved rate capability (337 mA h g-1 at 5 C) and excellent cycling stability (90% capacity retention after 400 cycles).  The superior electrochem. performances of the Sb-C nanofibers are due to the unique nanofiber structure and uniform distribution of Sb nanoparticles in carbon matrix, which provides a conductive and buffering matrix for effective release of mech. stress caused by Na ion insertion/extn. and prevent the aggregation of the Sb nanoparticles.</div></div><div class="moreSciFi"><a title="Retrieve detailed record, substances, reactions and more for this article from SciFinder ®" href="https://scifinder.cas.org/scifinder/view/link_v1/reference.jsf?l=BmxxGlm8wGqODsgQsiGAJrVg90H21EOLACvtfcHk0lgw1kg31UJJPg"> &gt;&gt; More from SciFinder <sup>®</sup></a></div><span class="casRefUrl">https://chemport.cas.org/services/resolver?origin=ACS&amp;resolution=options&amp;coi=1%3ACAS%3A528%3ADC%252BC3sXhvFKhtrrN&amp;md5=b043a6265ebe5b5183098fbd4c98cc1f</span></div></div></div></div></li></ol></li><li id="pane-m3" aria-labelledby="pane-m3" class="tab__pane tab__pane-suppInfo"><h2 class="supp-info-label">Supporting Information</h2><div class="article_supporting-info" id="rightTab-notes-1"><div class="article_content-header"><div class="article_content-header-row"><div class="article_content-title" tabindex="0"><h2 id="rightTab-_i8">Supporting Information</h2></div></div></div><hr><p class="last">The Supporting Information is available free of charge on the <a href="/" class="ext-link">ACS Publications website</a> at DOI: <a href="/doi/abs/10.1021/acsami.6b16000" class="ext-link">10.1021/acsami.6b16000</a>.</p><ul class="NLM_list-list_type-label" id="silist"><li><p class="inline">SEM images, TEM image, and HRTEM image of NVP, nitrogen adsorption/desorption isotherms of the NVP or NVP@rGO composites, cycling performance of the NVP@rGO electrode, typical discharge–charge profile of Sb/C composite, cycling performance of the Sb/C electrode, and the Sb/C//NVP@rGO sodium ion battery (<a href="/doi/suppl/10.1021/acsami.6b16000/suppl_file/am6b16000_si_001.pdf" class="ext-link">PDF</a>)</p></li></ul><p></p><div class="supInfoBoxOnFTP "><div class="sup-info-attachments"><ul><li><a class="suppl-anchor" href="/doi/suppl/10.1021/acsami.6b16000/suppl_file/am6b16000_si_001.pdf">am6b16000_si_001.pdf (1.57 MB)</a></li></ul></div></div><div id="rightTab-figshare-widget"></div><br><div class="TermsAndConditionsDropzoneRight" data-pb-dropzone="TermsAndConditionsDropzoneRight"><div data-widget-def="UX3HTMLWidget" data-widget-id="b84e6b6c-b4d0-4427-b286-3cf14d52d013" class="mb-4">

                <a title="Abstract" class="article__jump__link internalNav" href="#Abstract" data-id="article_stickyheader_JumpTo_Abstract">
                   <span>Abstract</span>
                </a>
            </li>
            <li>
                <a title="1 Introduction" class="article__jump__link internalNav" href="#_i1" data-id="article_stickyheader_JumpTo_1%20Introduction">
                   <span>1 Introduction</span>
                </a>

        <script nonce="90f6e84b9ab8775c-LHR">
(function(){
	
	/*Event Tracking for RIS menu dropdown - Article pages*/

	$('.cit-download-dropdown_button').on('click',function(e)
	{	
		e.preventDefault();
	    gtag('event', 'Export', { 'event_category': 'Citation', 'event_label':'Main'});

	});


	$('.cit-download-dropdown_content ul li').on('click',function(e)
	{	
	//	e.preventDefault();
	    var idx = $(this).index();
	    
	    var label = '';
	    if (idx === 0 ) {
	    	label = 'Citation';
	    } else if (idx === 1 ) {
	    	label = 'Abstract';
	    } else if (idx === 2 ) {
	    	label = 'Reference';
	    } else if (idx === 3 ) {
	    	label = 'More Options';
	    }
	   
	   gtag('event', 'Export', { 'event_category': 'Citation', 'event_label':label});
	});

	$('.header_contnav-next a').on('click', function(e){
        e.preventDefault();
        gtag('event', 'Top', { 'event_category': 'Article', 'event_label':'Right Arrow'});
	}); 

 	$('.header_contnav-pre a').on('click', function(e){
	    e.preventDefault();
	     gtag('event', 'Top', { 'event_category': 'Article', 'event_label':'Left Arrow'});
	}); 

	$('.share_button').on('click', function(e){
		e.preventDefault();
		gtag('event', 'Top', { 'event_category': 'Article', 'event_label':'Share'});
	});

	$("#pane-m1con").on('click', function(e) {
		e.preventDefault();
		gtag('event', 'Sidebar', { 'event_category': 'Article', 'event_label':'Figures'});
	});

	$("#pane-m2con").on('click', function(e) {
		e.preventDefault();
	    gtag('event', 'Sidebar', { 'event_category': 'Article', 'event_label':'References'});
	});

	$("#pane-m3con").on('click', function(e) {
		e.preventDefault();
		gtag('event', 'Sidebar', { 'event_category': 'Article', 'event_label':'Supporting Info'});
	});

	$('.tab__close').on('click', function(){
		gtag('event', 'Sidebar', { 'event_category': 'Article', 'event_label':'Close'});
	}); 



})();

</script>

        <p>Please be aware that pubs.acs.org is undergoing maintenance from Saturday February 1 to Monday Febraury 3, that may have an impact on your experience. <script nonce="90f6e84b9ab8775c-LHR">
    document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function(){
    // Function to get a Human readable formatted date
    function getFormattedDateForMaintenance() {
        let today = new Date();
        let dd = String(today.getDate()).padStart(2, '0');
        //January is 0
        let mm = String(today.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0'); 
        let yyyy = today.getFullYear();
        
        let daysOfWeek = ['Sunday', 'Monday', 'Tuesday', 'Wednesday', 'Thursday', 'Friday', 'Saturday'];
        let monthsOfYear = ['January', 'February', 'March', 'April', 'May', 'June', 'July', 'August', 'September', 'October', 'November', 'December'];

        let dayOfWeek = daysOfWeek[today.getDay()];
        let monthOfYear = monthsOfYear[today.getMonth()];

        return dayOfWeek + ', ' + monthOfYear + ' ' + dd + ', ' + yyyy;
    }
    
    // Insert the date into the .system-message-date element
    document.querySelector('.system-message-date').innerText = getFormattedDateForMaintenance();
});
</script>

<script type="text/javascript" nonce="90f6e84b9ab8775c-LHR">
"use strict"
//Script checks gdpr cookie and submits form
	/* 
	Create an in-page pop-up message, only for the InfoCentral homepage, that will gather email registrants for the library marketing list.
	 
	Needs the end point
	*/

var infoCentralCapture = (function() {

    //Detect mobile device
    window.mobilecheck = function() {
        var check = false;
        (function(a){if(/(android|bb\d+|meego).+mobile|avantgo|bada\/|blackberry|blazer|compal|elaine|fennec|hiptop|iemobile|ip(hone|od)|iris|kindle|lge |maemo|midp|mmp|mobile.+firefox|netfront|opera )|avan|be(ck|ll|nq)|bi(lb|rd)|bl(ac|az)|br(e|v)w|bumb|bw\-(n|u)|c55\/|capi|ccwa|cdm\-|cell|chtm|cldc|cmd\-|co(mp|nd)|craw|da(it|ll|ng)|dbte|dc\-s|devi|dica|dmob|do(c|p)o|ds(12|\-d)|el(49|ai)|em(l2|ul)|er(ic|k0)|esl8|ez([4-7]0|os|wa|ze)|fetc|fly(\-|_)|g1 u|g560|gene|gf\-5|g\-mo|go(\.w|od)|gr(ad|un)|haie|hcit|hd\-(m|p|t)|hei\-|hi(pt|ta)|hp( i|ip)|hs\-c|ht(c(\-| |_|a|g|p|s|t)|tp)|hu(aw|tc)|i\-(20|go|ma)|i230|iac( |\-|\/)|ibro|idea|ig01|ikom|im1k|inno|ipaq|iris|ja(t|v)a|jbro|jemu|jigs|kddi|keji|kgt( |\/)|klon|kpt |kwc\-|kyo(c|k)|le(no|xi)|lg( g|\/(k|l|u)|50|54|\-[a-w])|libw|lynx|m1\-w|m3ga|m50\/|ma(te|ui|xo)|mc(01|21|ca)|m\-cr|me(rc|ri)|mi(o8|oa|ts)|mmef|mo(01|02|bi|de|do|t(\-| |o|v)|zz)|mt(50|p1|v )|mwbp|mywa|n10[0-2]|n20[2-3]|n30(0|2)|n50(0|2|5)|n7(0(0|1)|10)|ne((c|m)\-|on|tf|wf|wg|wt)|nok(6|i)|nzph|o2im|op(ti|wv)|oran|owg1|p800|pan(a|d|t)|pdxg|pg(13|\-([1-8]|c))|phil|pire|pl(ay|uc)|pn\-2|po(ck|rt|se)|prox|psio|pt\-g|qa\-a|qc(07|12|21|32|60|\-[2-7]|i\-)|qtek|r380|r600|raks|rim9|ro(ve|zo)|s55\/|sa(ge|ma|mm|ms|ny|va)|sc(01|h\-|oo|p\-)|sdk\/|se(c(\-|0|1)|47|mc|nd|ri)|sgh\-|shar|sie(\-|m)|sk\-0|sl(45|id)|sm(al|ar|b3|it|t5)|so(ft|ny)|sp(01|h\-|v\-|v )|sy(01|mb)|t2(18|50)|t6(00|10|18)|ta(gt|lk)|tcl\-|tdg\-|tel(i|m)|tim\-|t\-mo|to(pl|sh)|ts(70|m\-|m3|m5)|tx\-9|up(\.b|g1|si)|utst|v400|v750|veri|vi(rg|te)|vk(40|5[0-3]|\-v)|vm40|voda|vulc|vx(52|53|60|61|70|80|81|83|85|98)|w3c(\-| )|webc|whit|wi(g |nc|nw)|wmlb|wonu|x700|yas\-|your|zeto|zte\-/i.test(a.substr(0,4))) check = true;})(navigator.userAgent||navigator.vendor||window.opera);
              return check;
        };

    var _isMobile = window.mobilecheck();
    if (_isMobile) {
        $('#gdpr-message-modal').addClass('mobile');
    }

    var emailValid = "",
        time = 3000,
        btnStatus = true,
        errorStatus = false,
        errormessage = "<p class='gdpr_err'><b>Please Enter a valid email address<b><p>";

    function init() {
        setTimeout(function() {
            var cookieExist = getCookie("gdpr");
            if (cookieExist) {
                //console.log("gdpr cookie exist");
                return false;
            } else {
                //console.log("gdpr cookie does not exist")
                gdprMessage();
            }
            //Events
            $('#closebtn').on("click", hideForm);

            //Handle submit
            $('#gdpr-message-btn').on("click", function(event) {
                handleClick();
            });

            // //Hide if clicked outside div - TO DO stop handling click after submit
            // $(document).click(function(event) {
            // 	event.stopPropagation();
            //   console.log(event.target);
            //   if (!$(event.target).closest("#gdpr-message-content").length) {
            //     $("body").find("#gdpr-message-modal").hide();
            //     $(this).off();
            //   }
            // });
            $('#gdpr-con-btn').click(function() {
                setCookie("gdpr", "true");
                hideForm();
            });
        }, time);
    }

    //Show the message
    function gdprMessage() {
        //console.log("Show GDPR Message");
        var tMessage, emailInput, messageButton, ewrap;

        $('#gdpr-message-modal').show();
    }

    function handleClick() {
        //console.log($("#gdpr-input").val());
        emailValid = validateEmail($("#gdpr-input").val());
        if (emailValid) {
            //Submit the form
            //Hide form
            if ($('.gdpr_err')) {
                $('.gdpr_err').hide();
            }

            $("#gdpr-message-content")
                //If successful then...
            setCookie("gdpr", "true");
            //console.log("emailValid " + emailValid + " submiting form");
        } else {
            //Show error message
            gdprErrorMessage();
            //console.log("emailValid " + emailValid);
        }
    }

    function gdprErrorMessage() {
        if (errorStatus) {
            return false;
        } else {
            errorStatus = true;
            $("#gdpr-message-content").append(errormessage);
        }
    }

    function validateEmail(email) {
        var re = /^(([^<>()\[\]\\.,;:\s@"]+(\.[^<>()\[\]\\.,;:\s@"]+)*)|(".+"))@((\[[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\])|(([a-zA-Z\-0-9]+\.)+[a-zA-Z]{2,}))$/;
        return re.test(String(email).toLowerCase());
    }

    function setCookie(name, value) {
        var expires = "";
        expires = "; expires=Fri, 31 Dec 9999 23:59:59 GMT";
        document.cookie = name + "=" + (value || "") + expires + "; path=/";
    }

    function getCookie(name) {
        var match = document.cookie.match(new RegExp(name + '=([^;]+)'));
        if (match) return match[1];
    }

    function hideForm() { //And set cookie
        $('#gdpr-message-modal').hide();
        setCookie("gdpr", "false");
        gtag('event', 'GDPR Modal', { 'event_category': 'Pubs GDPR', 'event_label':'GDPR Dismissal'});
    }

    return {
        init: init
    }
})();

$(document).ready(infoCentralCapture.init);
</script>


                    
                        



        
        <script nonce="90f6e84b9ab8775c-LHR">
var currentJournal = "ACS Applied Materials &amp;amp; Interfaces";
$(".citationLinks > a").click(function(e){
    if($(this).text() === "ACS Full Text ") {
        gtag('event', 'ACS Full Text', { 'event_category': 'Reference _Click', 'event_label':currentJournal});
    }
    else if($(this).text() === "Crossref") {
        gtag('event', 'Crossref', { 'event_category': 'Reference _Click', 'event_label':currentJournal});
    }
    else if($(this).text() === "CAS") {
        gtag('event', 'CAS', { 'event_category': 'Reference _Click', 'event_label':currentJournal});
    }
    else if($(this).text() === "PubMed") {
        gtag('event', 'PubMed', { 'event_category': 'Reference _Click', 'event_label':currentJournal});
    }
    else if($(this).text() === "Google Scholar") {
        gtag('event', 'Google Scholar', { 'event_category': 'Reference _Click', 'event_label':currentJournal});
    }
    else if($(this).hasClass("issue-item_open-url") === true) {
        gtag('event', 'OpenURL', { 'event_category': 'Reference _Click', 'event_label':currentJournal});
    }
});
</script>
